<div class="dkl-bg ad" id="dkls"></div>
<!-- dkls -->
<script type="text/javascript">
  var str_kls_url = 'https://img.lrytas.lt/dklausimas/';
  var dksl_bals = 0;
  var q_id = 0;

  function createCookie(name,value,days) {
    if (days) {
      var date = new Date();
      date.setTime(date.getTime()+(days*24*60*60*1000));
      var expires = "; expires="+date.toGMTString();
    } else {
      var expires = "";
    }
    document.cookie = name+"="+value+expires+"; path=/";
  }

function readCookie(name) {
  var nameEQ = name + "=";
  var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
  for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {
    var c = ca[i];
    while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);
    if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) {
      return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
    }
  }
  return 0;
}

function updv(r,u) {
  var notice = jQuery('#dkls');
  if (typeof(r) == 'object') {
    q_id = r.id;
    var balsavo = readCookie('kl' + q_id);
    notice.html('');
    var s = '';
    if (u == 1 || balsavo) {
      createCookie('kl' + q_id,1,60);

      s = '<div class="box6-head"></div>\
      <div class="box11">\
        <form id="myform" onsubmit="return false">\
          <div class="quest">' + r.k + '</div>\
          <table style="background-color:transparent;">';
          } else {
            s = '<div class="box6-head">\
            <div class="box6-meniu"></div>\
          </div>\
          <div class="box11">\
            <form id="myform" onsubmit="return false">\
              <div class="quest">' + r.k + '</div>';
            }

            for(var i = 0; i < r.a.length; i++) {
              var nr = i + 1;
              if (u == 1 || balsavo) {
                s += '<tr>\
                <td class="txt" colspan=2>\
                  <p class="text-13">' + r.a[i] + '</p>\
                  <div><div style="float:left;width:' + r.i[i] + 'px;height:15px;background-color:#0068B4;margin-right:4px">\
                    <img src="//img.lrytas.lt/img/p.gif" width=' + r.i[i] + ' height=15 /></div><div style="float:left"><p class="text-13">' + r.r[i] + ' (' + r.p[i] + '%) </p></div></div>\
                  </td>\
                </tr>';
              } else {
                s += '<div class="q-line">\
                <div class="radio"><input type="radio" name="vienas" value="' + nr + '"/></div>\
                <div class="klausimas">' + r.a[i] + '</div>\
              </div>';
            }
          }

          if (u == 1 || balsavo) {
            s += '<tr><td colspan=2 class="td_rez_viso"><p class="text-13">Iš viso balsavo: ' + r.v + '</p></td></tr></table></form></div></div>';
          } else {
            s += '<div class="submits">\
            <a href="javascript:void(0)" onclick="javascript:addv(jQuery(\'#myform input[name=vienas]:checked\').val());return true;"><img src="//img.lrytas.lt/css2/img/bg-balsuoti.png" /></a>\
          </div>\
        </form>\
      </div>\
    </div>';
  }

  notice.html(s);
  notice.hide();
  var redrawFix = notice.offsetHeight;
  notice.show();
}
}

function addv(n) { 
  if (typeof n == "undefined") { return true; }
  if (n < 1 || q_id == 0) { return true; }
  if (dksl_bals == 0) {
    var notice = jQuery('#dkls');
    notice.html('<div style="height:100px;width:190px" /><img src="//img.lrytas.lt/img/indicator.gif" style="display:block;margin:auto;margin-top:45px" /></div>');
    dksl_bals = 1;
	jQuery.ajax({
		url: str_kls_url,
		dataType: 'json',
		data: { kls_id: q_id, v: n },
		cache: false,
		success: function (data) {
			updv(data,1);
		}
		
	}
	);

}

		url: str_kls_url,
		dataType: 'json',
		data: { tema: 0 },
		cache: false,
		success: function (data) {
			updv(data,0);
			if (data.length != 0) {
				jQuery('#dkls').fadeIn();
			}
		}
		
	}
	);

Lietuvos biomasės energetikos asociacijos LITBIOMA direktorė Vilma Gaubytė sako, kad Lietuvos įmonės nėra pajėgios konkuruoti su baltarusiška biokuro kaina ir yra priverstos užsidaryti.

<script type="text/javascript">
//		console.info('show');
var main_b_order = b_order.slice(0);
 function createCookie(name,value,days) {
    if (days) {
      var date = new Date();
      date.setTime(date.getTime()+(days*24*60*60*1000));
      var expires = "; expires="+date.toGMTString();
    } else {
      var expires = "";
    }
    document.cookie = name+"="+value+expires+"; path=/";
  }

function readCookie(name) {
  var nameEQ = name + "=";
  var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
  for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {
    var c = ca[i];
    while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);
    if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) {
      return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
    }
  }
  return 0;
}
var lr_cookie_name = "lrorder_kolumbus6";
function fp_show_first () {
  var s = ''; var tmp = new Array();
  for (var i = 0; i < b_order.length; i++)
  { if (i == 0) {
      jQuery("#t_p_" + b_order[i]).insertBefore(jQuery("#t_p_main").children().first());
    }
    else {
      jQuery("#t_p_" + b_order[i]).insertAfter(jQuery("#t_p_" + b_order[i-1]));
    }
    
    //tmp.push($('t_p_' + b_order[i]).remove());
    }
	jQuery('#t_p_main').find("div[data-cx='1']").each(function(index,div) {
		var id = jQuery(div).attr('id');
		jQuery(div).html('');
		var cxid = id.replace(/^div_/, '');
		setTimeout(function () { cxAdv.draw({ 'id': cxid, 'div_id':id }); }, 25);
	});
  //$('t_p_main').innerHTML = '';
  //tmp.each(function (e) { $('t_p_main').appendChild(e); });
  //v_karuseles.each(function (e) { if (typeof e.first == 'function') { e.next();e.first();} });

}

var b_tvarka = readCookie(lr_cookie_name);
//var b_order = new Array();
if (b_tvarka == 0){
	createCookie(lr_cookie_name, main_b_order.slice(0).join(), 365*10);
	b_order = main_b_order.slice(0);
}
else
{ b_order = b_tvarka.split(',');
  
  var cmp_array = main_b_order.slice(0);
  var t = b_order.slice(0); var t2 = cmp_array.slice(0);
  if (t.sort().join() != t2.sort().join())
  { // atsirado/dingo blokai
       b_order = cmp_array.slice(0);
       createCookie(lr_cookie_name, b_order.join(), 365*10);
  }
  fp_show_first();
}
function fp_order(n, d)
{ console.info('fp_order ' + n + ' ' + d );
var ai = -1;
 for (var i = 0; i <b_order.length && ai < 1; i++)
 { if (b_order[i] == n){
 ai = i;
 }
 }
 if (ai <0 || (ai == 0 && d == 'up') || (ai == b_order.length - 1 && d == 'down') ) { return; }
 // console.info('buvo: ' + b_order.join() + ' gavau ' + n + ' ' + d);
 if (d == 'up')
 { var tmp = b_order[ai - 1];
 var div1 =  jQuery('#t_p_' + b_order[ai]);
 var div2 = jQuery('#t_p_' + tmp);
 b_order[ai - 1] = b_order[ai];
 b_order[ai] = tmp;
 div1.insertBefore(div2);
 div1.find("div[data-cx='1']").each(function(index,div) {
		var id = jQuery(div).attr('id');
		jQuery(div).html('');
		var cxid = id.replace(/^div_/, '');
		setTimeout(function () { cxAdv.draw({ 'id': cxid, 'div_id':id }); }, 25);
	});

 console.info('block up');
 }
 if (d == 'down')
 { var tmp = b_order[ai + 1];
 var div1 =  jQuery('#t_p_' + b_order[ai]);
 var div2 = jQuery('#t_p_' + tmp);
 div1.insertAfter(div2);
 div1.find("div[data-cx='1']").each(function(index,div) {
		var id = jQuery(div).attr('id');
		jQuery(div).html('');
		var cxid = id.replace(/^div_/, '');
		setTimeout(function () { cxAdv.draw({ 'id': cxid, 'div_id':id }); }, 25);
	});
 b_order[ai + 1] = b_order[ai];
 b_order[ai] = tmp;
 console.info('block down');
 }
 createCookie(lr_cookie_name, b_order.join(), 365*10);
 console.info('yra: ' + b_order.join());
 //fp_show_first();
}
